)@@G@@OR ITS OPERANDS; THIS IS CALLED ITS 'DOMAIN', AND AN  @F@@@@ ATTEMPT TO QJ
)@@G@@VIOLATE THESE RULES WILL RESULT IN A 'DOMAIN ERROR'.  @F@@@@ AS AN EXAMPQK

)@@G@@ . QW-IN    @I@@@@.         THE FOLLOWING ROUTINE ENABLES TTY35 TO BYPASEB
)@@G@@S THE TRANSLATION  . QW-IN    @I@@@@.         OF INPUT CHARACTERS INTO FEC
)@@G@@IELDATA THAT NORMALLY OCCURS BEFORE  . QW-IN    @I@@@@.         THEY AREED
)@@G@@ PASSED ON TO A PROGRAM.                               . QW-IN    @I@@@@EE
)@@G@@.                                                                       EF

)@@G@@, CONTROL GOES     . QW-IN    @I@@@@.         TO QWDMOD.  IF THE DEVICE EH
)@@G@@IS NOT ELIGIBLE FOR UNTRANSLATED     . QW-IN    @I@@@@.         INPUT, CEI
)@@G@@ONTROL RETURNS TO NORMAL PROCESSING OF A 'SO'.  IF     . QW-IN    @I@@@@EJ
)@@G@@.         THE DEVICE IS ELIGIBLE, QWFLAG IS SET AND 077 IS STORED AS THEEK
)@@G@@ . QW-IN    @I@@@@.         NEXT FIELDATA CHARACTER IN THE INPUT IMAGE. EL
)@@G@@ THE LOW ORDER     . QW-IN    @I@@@@.         SEVEN BITS OF SUBSEQUENT CEM
)@@G@@HARACTERS ARE STORED IN SUCCESSIVE   . QW-IN    @I@@@@.         QUARTER EN
)@@G@@WORDS FOLLOWING THE 077.  THE IMAGE IS SENT TO THE     . QW-IN    @I@@@@EO
)@@G@@.         USER WHENEVER THE 14 WORD BUFFER IS FILLED OR WHENEVER A      EP

)@@G@@STORED IN THE      . QW-IN    @I@@@@.         IMAGE.  SUBSEQUENT IMAGE WER
)@@G@@ILL HAVE 0777 AS Q1 OF THE FIRST     . QW-IN    @I@@@@.         WORD TO ES
